{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Real\+Type $>$ \\
std\+::int64\+\_\+t \mbox{\hyperlink{classcompnal_1_1model_1_1_base_u1_electron__1_d}{compnal\+::model\+::\+Base\+U1\+Electron\+\_\+1D}}$<$ Real\+Type $>$\+::Calculate\+Target\+Dim (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::pair$<$ int, double $>$ \&}]{quantum\+\_\+number }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Calculate the dimension of the target Hilbert space specified by the system size $ N$, the number of the total electrons $ \langle\hat{N}_{\rm e}\rangle$, and the total sz $ \langle\hat{S}^{z}_{\rm tot}\rangle $. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em quantum\+\_\+number} & The pair of the total electron $ \langle\hat{N}_{\rm e}\rangle $ and total sz $ \langle\hat{S}^{z}_{\rm tot}\rangle$ \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The dimension of the target Hilbert space. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{compnal::model::BaseU1Electron\_1D$<$ RealType $>$@{compnal::model::BaseU1Electron\_1D$<$ RealType $>$}!CreateOnsiteOperatoriSy@{CreateOnsiteOperatoriSy}}
\index{CreateOnsiteOperatoriSy@{CreateOnsiteOperatoriSy}!compnal::model::BaseU1Electron\_1D$<$ RealType $>$@{compnal::model::BaseU1Electron\_1D$<$ RealType $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CreateOnsiteOperatoriSy()}{CreateOnsiteOperatoriSy()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Real\+Type $>$ \\
static \mbox{\hyperlink{structcompnal_1_1sparse__matrix_1_1_c_r_s}{CRS}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcompnal_1_1model_1_1_base_u1_electron__1_d}{compnal\+::model\+::\+Base\+U1\+Electron\+\_\+1D}}$<$ Real\+Type $>$\+::Create\+Onsite\+Operatori\+Sy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}



Generate the spin operator for the y-\/direction for the electrons $ i\hat{s}^{y}=\frac{1}{2}(\hat{c}^{\dagger}_{\uparrow}\hat{c}_{\downarrow} - \hat{c}^{\dagger}_{\downarrow}\hat{c}_{\uparrow})$. Here $ i=\sqrt{-1}$ is the the imaginary unit. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
